<div id="review_139939856" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/139939856" />
    <a title="Brianna (The Book Vixen)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2125148-brianna-the-book-vixen"><img alt="Brianna (The Book Vixen)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377917104p2/2125148.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/139939856?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brianna (The Book Vixen)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brianna (The Book Vixen)" href="/user/show/2125148-brianna-the-book-vixen">Brianna (The Book Vixen)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781402245770" href="/book/show/9421637-rock-hard">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2125148-brianna-the-book-vixen?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2125148-brianna-the-book-vixen?shelf=_cb">_cb</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer139939856" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer282305549000639477"><i>Review copy provided by publisher</i><br/><br/><b>Why I Read this Book:</b> This series is my new guilty pleasure. I’m new to the world of Contemporary Erotic Romance so I was a bit wary at first. But after reading <i>Backstage Pass</i>, I’m hooked! <i>Rock Hard</i> is the 2nd book in the Sinners series and it’s Sed’s (the lead singer of the Sinners) story.<br/><br/><b>What I Liked:</b> It feels like I’m reading an autobiography of a real-life rock band. It’s scary how real these characters feel. This is the type of book that I enjoy reading beca</span>
  <span id="freeText282305549000639477" style="display:none"><i>Review copy provided by publisher</i><br /><br /><b>Why I Read this Book:</b> This series is my new guilty pleasure. I’m new to the world of Contemporary Erotic Romance so I was a bit wary at first. But after reading <i>Backstage Pass</i>, I’m hooked! <i>Rock Hard</i> is the 2nd book in the Sinners series and it’s Sed’s (the lead singer of the Sinners) story.<br /><br /><b>What I Liked:</b> It feels like I’m reading an autobiography of a real-life rock band. It’s scary how real these characters feel. This is the type of book that I enjoy reading because it lets me live in someone else’s shoes, if only for a few hundred pages. It’s like being a groupie except without having any of the consequences.<br /><br />The book focuses on the main hero and heroine but the reader also gets to see what’s going on with the rest of the band members as well. Each band mate’s story continues from the first book to the next and we see that being demonstrated in <i>Rock Hard</i>. We get to see what’s going on with Brian and Myrna. It was nice to catch up with them and see what they’ve been up to. Jace was definitely enjoying himself in this book. I thought it was a nice setup to his book, which is coming next. Methinks there’ll be a little – okay, probably a lot – of BDSM going on in his book. The guy does love his “accessories”.<br /><br /><b>What I Didn’t Like:</b> I am not a fan of Sed’s; he is my least favorite character in the group. He was an ass in the first book and he’s still an ass in this book. Sed was extremely unpleasant and at times, annoying. He means well, he just doesn’t do it in a proper manner.<br /><br />I was more tuned in to what was going on in the secondary story arcs than I was with Sed and Jessica; they took a back burner for me. There was a major lack of communication between the two of them. When they’re weren’t fighting, they were having sex (and vice-versa). Lots of sex and lots of fighting.<br /><br />One part I thought was a bit peculiar was that it was Sed and Jessica who knew what was going on with Trey’s…situation. Even Myrna wasn’t accepting the reality of the situation and that was a bit strange to me.<br /><br /><b>Overall Impression:</b> Even though I didn’t enjoy <i>Rock Hard</i> as much as I did <i>Backstage Pass</i>, it was still a good read. This series has proved to be a fascinating inside look at the lives of a rock band. Fans of the movie Rock Star, with Mark Wahlberg and Jennifer Aniston, will enjoy reading this series. I gave <i>Backstage Pass</i> a 4/5 rating and thought it was a great debut novel. <i>Rock Hard</i> was good but Sed just drove me nuts. I just wasn’t feeling his story like I did Brian’s. I’m definitely looking forward to the next book, <i>Hot Ticket</i>, which is Jace’s book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="282305549000639477" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>

</a>

    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4tGc6diFYDaF6qP6Q/xujnybhhCUdLNZ62qonBNklK3iyZIxji/dj7sp+06/86SEtns+DHJItYP9/Jai++mjGA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dCwQrt7SLnDN2DnnqHQxfJIEBA7UUyxqAtbEuorBN1R0NB52iHiTyfMbYVNUe/t2WOS8EjJvKrAUQPqEYkwA4Q==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer8146410354501705734">Combining her love for romantic fiction and rock ‘n roll, Olivia Cunning writes erotic romance centered around rock musicians. Raised on hard rock music from the cradle, she attended her first Styx concert at age six and fell instantly in love with live music. She's been known to travel over a thousand miles just to see a favorite band in concert. As a teen, she discovered her second love, romanti</span>
  <span id="freeText8146410354501705734" style="display:none">Combining her love for romantic fiction and rock ‘n roll, Olivia Cunning writes erotic romance centered around rock musicians. Raised on hard rock music from the cradle, she attended her first Styx concert at age six and fell instantly in love with live music. She's been known to travel over a thousand miles just to see a favorite band in concert. As a teen, she discovered her second love, romantic fiction -- first, voraciously reading steamy romance novels and then penning her own. Growing up as the daughter of a career soldier, she's lived all over the country and overseas. She recently moved to Galveston, Texas.</span>
